<div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden">
    	
            <h3>Valley Metro</h3>
<p>Valley Metro plans, develops and operates the regional bus and light rail systems and alternative transportation programs for commuters, seniors and people with disabilities. We exist to connect communities and enhance lives.</p>
<p>
</p><div id="block-menu-menu-about" class="block block-menu">
<div class="content">

<li class="leaf depth--1 is-hiding-child-items"><a href="/sustainability" title="">Sustainability</a></li>
<li class="last leaf depth--1 is-hiding-child-items"><a href="/strategic-plan">Strategic Plan</a></li>
</ul></div>
